				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Orchestral Suite No.2 in B minor, BWV 1067 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1738–39
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Suites&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Suites</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Overtures&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Overtures</a></span>;
